Important News 2

Results of the Shandong Village Clearing Conference 80

The province is divided into six major districts and three minor districts

The work steps are to first suppress bandits and then clear the villages

Jinan Correspondence: Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government and Shandong-Henan Village Clearing Supervisor, specially convened the division commanders to Jinan to hold a bandit suppression conference in order to plan the village clearing in the province. Last night (11th) at 6:00 pm, after the 20th Division Commander Sun Tongxuan came to Jinan from Zhoucun Defense Zone, the bandit suppression conference was held at the General Headquarters at 7:00 pm that night. Those who attended included Zhang Yue, Director of the Counselor's Office of the Village Clearing Supervisor's Office, Li Zongbi, Chief of Staff of the General Headquarters, and the directors of various departments, 20th Division Commander Sun Tongxuan, 29th Division Commander Cao Fulin, 22nd Division Commander Gu Liangmin, 74th Division Commander Qiao Lizhi, and 81st Division Commander Zhan Shutang. Chairman Han Fuju presided over the meeting and decided that each division would launch a large-scale bandit suppression campaign in its respective area, limited to two months to clear the bandits. The province is divided into six districts and three small districts. The area near Jinan is one district, which is the responsibility of 74th Division Commander Qiao Lizhi. The Jinan business district is the responsibility of Lei Taiping, the commander of the Pistol Brigade. The area east of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway and along the Jiaoji Railway (Zhoucun Weixian) north to Huimin in northern Shandong is one district, which is said to be centered on Zouping and is the responsibility of 20th Division Commander Sun Tongxuan. Northern Shandong (west of Huimin) and western Shandong are one district, which is the responsibility of 29th Division Commander Cao Fulin and Cavalry Brigade Commander Li Xuande. Southern Shandong, including Linyi, Tancheng, Feixian, and Yishui, is one district, which is the responsibility of 80th Division Commander Zhan Shutang. Taian, Yanzhou, Jining, and Caozhou are one district, which is the responsibility of 22nd Division Commander Gu Liangmin. Eastern Shandong, east of Weixian, is one district, which is the responsibility of Liu Zhennian, Commander of the Central 21st Division. The three small districts are: Linqing is one district, which is the responsibility of Zhao Renquan, Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Shandong Republic; Jining is one district, which is the responsibility of Gu Liangyou, Commander-in-Chief of the Western Shandong Militia; and the area around Xintai is one district, which is the responsibility of Xie Shuxian, Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Shandong Militia. The above three small districts are affiliated troops and are subject to the command of the large district where they are located. The conference also decided to carry out village clearing after the bandits in the province are eliminated. The conference also agreed on the steps for bandit suppression, planning to use the troops of Gu Liangmin and Zhan Shutang to jointly suppress the bandits Guo Mafeng and Liu Guitang in Mengshan, Baodugu, and other places in southern Shandong. Ma Hongkui's 15th Route Army was originally stationed in the area of Taian, Lincheng, Tengxian, Zaozhuang, Linbo, and Jining. Now, Ma's troops have been ordered to be transferred to Henan. Gu Liangmin's troops will fill the defense. Gu's Ning Chunxiao Brigade is now stationed in Jining, Qufu, and Sishui. Tang Kesun Brigade is now stationed in Tengxian and Juancheng. The division headquarters and independent battalions are stationed in Yanzhou (now stationed in Weixian, Qingzhou, Jiaoxian, and Gaomi). Zhan Shutang's troops will be transferred to defend Linyi, Yishui, Feixian, and Tancheng. The division headquarters will be located in Linyi. The Yun Qichang Brigade of the division stationed in Jiaoxian will be transferred from Jiaoxian to Linyi and Tancheng via Zhucheng and Juxian. Zhan Shutang will lead the division headquarters and independent units from Weixian to Linyi via Anqiu and Juxian. The Tang Bangzhi Brigade stationed in Qingzhou will be transferred from Linqu to Yishui and Feixian. After the two divisions arrive at their destinations, they will begin to jointly suppress the bandits in Mengshan and Baodugu. The troops of Cao Fulin, who is responsible for the area west of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway on the north bank of the Yellow River, are now stationed in Jinan. The Li Hanzhang Brigade of the division is stationed between Dezhou and Jinan. The Chen Dexin Brigade is stationed in Dongchang and Guantao. The Rong Guangxing Brigade will be transferred back to Jinan. The Cavalry Brigade Li Xuande is stationed in Xiajin and is responsible for the area east of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway and along the Jiaoji Railway on the north bank of the Yellow River. Sun Tongxuan's troops are stationed in Zhoucun. The Zhao Xinde Brigade of the division is now stationed in Zhanhua and Lijin. The Ma Jingong Brigade is stationed in Boshan. The 58th Brigade is stationed in Weixian with one regiment in Dexian. The Xie Shijie Artillery Regiment is also stationed in Dexian and is now transferred to Zhoucun, Qingzhou, and Weixian to fill the defense left by Zhan Shutang's troops. The division commanders are still in Jinan, claiming departure expenses and supplies. It is said that they will return to their defense zones within one or two days to prepare for departure. It is expected that they will arrive at their destinations around October 10 and begin to suppress bandits. This is because the busy farming season will have passed by then, and the militia can also help the government army suppress bandits. (September 12)

End of the First Fleet Naval Exercises 81

Fuzhou Correspondence: The First Fleet of the Navy, under the command of Chen Jiliang, sailed from Shanghai in the latter part of last month with ten warships, including the cruisers "Hai Chou" and "Hai Rong," the gunboats "Da Tong," "Zi Qiang," "Yu Zhang," "Yong Jian," "Yong Ji," and "Jian Kang," and the training ships "Tong Ji" and "Ying Rui," to conduct naval exercises in the waters off Fujian and Zhejiang. Starting from Sanduao and maneuvering to Xiangshan Harbor, they practiced heavy artillery firing, torpedo firing, and various maneuvers with submarine search formations along the way. These exercises have now concluded. On September 4th, he led all the ships to Xiamen, went ashore to inspect various modern constructions and historical sites in Xiamen, and attended banquets hosted by political and military circles. On the 8th, the entire fleet sailed to the province. At 11:00 AM on the 9th, they arrived at Mawei. Huang Maohe, the commander of the Marine Corps regiment, Shao Bin, the director of the Navy's provincial office, Mao Zhencai, the commander of the Changle Fort, and Jiang Zhizhuang, a staff officer of the Ministry of the Navy, all went aboard the cruiser "Hai Chou" to pay their respects to Commander Chen. On the evening of the 10th, Staff Officer Zheng, acting commander of the Mawei Naval Port Command, hosted a banquet for all the officers at the Navy's Recreation Club. Currently, Chen plans to lead the captains of each ship to the province on the 11th to visit Yang Shuzhuang at Guling and report on the exercises. After resting for a few days, he will lead the ships back to Shanghai and then to their original stations.

The "Jiang Yuan" transport ship, stationed along the Min River, sailed to Xiamen a few days ago to transport the Guangdong Provincial Security Force, consisting of the Huang Gu and Fan Zong units stationed in Tong'an, to Beijing for reorganization. While sailing through Xiaomai Island in the Xinghua waters, it struck a reef, and part of the hold was flooded, creating a very dangerous situation. It immediately sent out a wireless distress signal. Upon receiving the report, the Mawei Naval Port Command immediately dispatched the gunboat "Yong Ji" to the rescue, transferring the ship's officers and soldiers to the rescue vessel. The damaged ship is now being repaired by craftsmen. (September 11th)

Shanghai Soong Residents in Beijing Urge Immediate Repair of Jinshanwei Seawall 82

Recently, the seawalls in Jiangsu Province have repeatedly faced danger. The Baoshan seawall project is perceived to be extremely hazardous, and the Songjiang seawall has also shown repeated signs of damage. For the sake of preventing future disasters, people from various former Song Prefecture counties residing in Beijing have appealed to the provincial government to allocate funds and select personnel to quickly repair and reinforce the seawall. The telegram reads as follows: To Chairman Ye of the Jiangsu Provincial Government in Zhenjiang: The flood in Jiangsu Province has caused widespread disaster, with the situation in Jiangnan being slightly less severe than in Jiangbei. Although the former Song Prefecture counties have also suffered losses, they have fortunately avoided being submerged. However, the Jinshanwei seawall has been neglected for years, and sections two, three, and four have recently collapsed one after another. As the autumn tides will soon rise, if unforeseen circumstances occur, the coastal counties will again be entirely inundated. It is not only the people who mourn the loss of their fisheries, but the entire province of Jiangsu will have no clean land left. Thinking of our homeland, we tremble with fear. We urge you to allocate special funds and select personnel familiar with seawall construction to work with local officials to quickly repair and reinforce the seawall, thereby averting major disasters and ensuring the safety of the people. We humbly request your prompt action. The Standing Committee of the Shanghai Soong Residents Association in Beijing, Zhu Shuyuan, Huang Duanlu, and Xia Guangyu, respectfully petition.

(40) Record of a conversation with Luo (transliteration) on March 13 (regarding issues such as Spireddonov's (transliteration) trip north to prepare for worker struggles in factories and attempts to sabotage the National Army).

Spireddonov's (transliteration) report on his inspection trip north: The activities of the right-wing faction of the Communist Party have not only split the party but also the organization of the masses, which is very unfortunate. The right-leaning elements openly violate the interests of the workers and put forward anti-struggle slogans. The work of the trade union under the leadership of Li Lisan has not paid attention to this, so few railway workers are organized. Comrade, who used to be the leader of the railway workers' movement, has recently turned into an opportunist. There is almost no mass movement. As for Tianjin, there is even a lack of mass organization. Rong Nanchun (transliteration) previously wanted to use the party organization of the railway factory as the basis for his right-wing faction, but he was recently arrested. He had great influence in the Beijing-Ningbo Railway, with 130 to 140 workers under his command. Since his arrest, these workers have been trying to rescue him and collecting money to help him. We have seven trade union members in Changxindian on the Beijing-Hankou Railway, and there are also seventy or eighty people on the whole railway, but there is still a lack of proper organization. Railway workers have recently been very vocal in opposing dismissals and arrests. They also have a good understanding of the Red Army. Last November, they planned to convene a railway workers' conference in the White Area, but after receiving instructions, they changed it to the Red Area. At that time, many representatives participated, but because they could not return to their original places, they had to join the Red Army. Our current task is how to consolidate the foundation of railway workers, and we must exclude Rong and others before we can step up the daily struggle. The Northern Railway Workers' Union has recently sent a comrade to inspect the Beijing-Ningbo line. As for the Beijing-Hankou Railway, there are red trade union posters at every station, called "Locomotive." The comrade leading this work is Zhu Chuting (transliteration), who was sent by the National Labor Union. We are now planning to convene a conference of workers on the entire Beijing-Hankou Railway on April 1, but the date may be flexible because it will take some time to select representatives from various places (the conference is scheduled to last one day, with about ten representatives). We must carefully organize the original seventy or eighty people to make them an action group. This responsibility will also be borne by Comrade Zhu Chuting, who will plan and convene the conference. At present, the Railway Workers' Union must send ten people to the northern section to take on guidance work, and these people must be given short-term training in advance. The National Labor Union must also assign one person to Tianjin to take on this work. The best candidate would be the current core secretary of the National Labor Union (the reason why we are making such a suggestion is that this important work cannot be handled without someone with considerable ability). Luo (transliteration) said that he would personally go there to work for two weeks, but if the National Labor Union can find another suitable person, it would be better to send someone else. We have recently sent a comrade to Manchuria to organize a trade union (this person's name is Wang Qinyin, transliteration), but the workers there requested that a certain comrade who used to work on the Siberian Railway and is now in Liaoning be sent to lead them. Unfortunately, they did not mention the name, so it is impossible to verify. The Standing Committee of the National Labor Union is now planning to reorganize the Railway Workers' Committee and send new members to strengthen its forces. They decided to send ten students from the north to work in various factories in Tianjin (according to Spireddonov's (transliteration) report, it was submitted to the Central Political Bureau, so this decision is suspected to have come from that bureau). The comrade who used to work in the Tianjin Trade Union is now said to be assigned to work in the mining area, but this work originally belongs to the party's scope, so we must first obtain the party's permission before we can make a decision. We each have ten comrades working in the four major coal mines in Tianjin, but the right-wing faction is very active there, so a few comrades have been arrested. Moreover, because of the activities of the right-wing faction there, we cannot send more qualified comrades there, because they would be in danger of being exposed as soon as they arrived. Regarding the above report, the National Labor Union's future resolutions will still follow the opinions of the Political Bureau. However, since we have not yet organized a trade union in that area, what name will we use to call on the workers in that area to engage in struggle in the future is still a problem. Recently, two new comrades have returned here. One is the chairman of the Hong Kong Labor Union, who had to leave Hong Kong because his work there has recently encountered obstacles and plans to be sent to the Soviet district to work. The other person comes from Liaoning. They will have a detailed report in a few days. (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 84

A Thief Named A Cai Has Been Arrested The notorious thief Jiang A Cai repeatedly robbed in San Guan Tang, You Li, Cheng Shan, and other places in Zhejiang Province. Later, he used the alias Shen Rongjiang, and carrying the stolen goods, he hid in Suzhou City at No. 16 Jinshi River. The Third District of the Zhejiang Inland River Police learned from the captured thieves A Fu, A De, and Zhou A Si about Jiang's hiding place. They dispatched Detective Captain Pan Xiru, leading investigator Zhu Fulin, who came to Suzhou to meet with the second and fifth branch stations of the Public Security Bureau, and arrested Jiang at the address at 11:00 AM on the 14th. They also seized three leather suitcases, three wooden suitcases, one handbag, one tin suitcase, and one silk tent. He was temporarily detained at the Public Security Bureau, awaiting transfer for prosecution.

Bandits in Taihu Lake Are Rampant Again Villagers Zhou A Fu and Zhou Shenquan were sailing a boat of pigs into the city on the 14th when, passing the experimental rice field in Shili Ting, they were suddenly met by a bandit boat with five bandits on board, who attempted to rob them. The patrolling police Han Wendou and Sun Bingnan noticed and opened fire on the bandits. The bandits also returned fire with pistols. After holding out for half an hour, the bandits ran out of ammunition and fled. In addition, Zhuang Songqing of Caojiabang in Hengjing and the home of Shen Zumin in Wujiabang reported to the Eighth Public Security Bureau that bandits were planning to rob them, and police were dispatched to protect them. As a result, a bandit scout named Zhang Jindada was arrested and sent to the city. Furthermore, Lu Huiqing's son Chan Sheng and nephew Fu Bao from Dongxie Road of the town were on a boat when they encountered a bandit boat with seven or eight bandits, with a female bandit rowing the boat. The boat was full of guns of all kinds, and they kidnapped the two men along with the boat. Yesterday (the 14th), Lu came to the city to report and request rescue.

Changshu 85

The Water Conservancy Problems in the Fourth and Fifth Districts Have Been Resolved This year, there have been continuous rains in the summer and autumn, and water levels have risen everywhere, turning the fields into a vast expanse of water. The original San Gan River runs through the fourth and fifth districts of the county. Its upper reaches are Pucheng in the fifth district, and its lower reaches are Shazhou City in the fourth district. As the river flowed downstream, the fields of Shazhou were further damaged. Therefore, the farmers of Shazhou suddenly dug mud to build a dam at the southern end of the lower reaches of the San Gan River, preventing the water from flowing downstream. Once the river was blocked, the water could not flow through, which was very detrimental to the fifth district. Therefore, they gathered thousands of villagers and sent dozens of representatives to the county to petition. According to County Chief Tan, the fault lies with the fourth district, and they should be ordered to open the dam as soon as possible. However, the people of Shazhou refused, declaring that they would rather die in the ditch than give up their dam. As a result, the dam has not been opened, and it has been two months without a solution. On the 11th, County Chief Tan went to the countryside to inspect the disaster situation and also inspected the dam. He also confirmed that it was necessary to open it and ordered Zhu Qingnan, the head of the fourth district, to open the dam within three days, and left Inspector Lu of the Public Security Bureau to monitor the situation in the countryside. When the villagers heard about this, they immediately gathered thousands of farmers to surround the district office, demanding that the dam be stopped, otherwise they would gather and die on the dam. At that time, District Chief Zhu and Inspector Lu repeatedly persuaded them and agreed to hold a citizens' meeting to resolve the issue, and the villagers dispersed. The conference decided at Wujie Bridge on the 13th, and the citizens of Shazhou again requested District Chief Zhu to consider public opinion and not accept any conditions to remove the dam privately, and told him the reasons why it could not be removed, otherwise the villagers would have to gather and die on the dam. At that time, the farmers, with a large number of people, pushed out Liu Zhu-ru, Huang Bao-zhen, and Huang Jin-hu as representatives. After the meeting, they asked Yang Zai-tian, a merchant in the Shazhou district, to mediate. As a result, Tian Yang guaranteed to return the fourth district farmers' loss of hundreds of yuan for building the dam. They agreed to the removal of the dam, so work began on the 14th to remove the dam, in compliance with the county order.

A Fire in a Carpenter's Shop, the Fate of a Woman and Two Children Unknown A carpenter's shop was opened at No. 70 Dongzhong Lane in the county town, owned by a man named Xiang Ersi. There was a lot of wood in the house. At around 11:00 PM on the 13th, the apprentices and carpenters were all asleep. Unexpectedly, an apprentice named Dalang suddenly heard crackling sounds downstairs and got up to see flames burning brightly. He shouted wildly for the master, Zou Wen-sheng, who heard the noise and saw the flames, and immediately took the quilts and other items from the bed downstairs and fled. However, the fire was so fierce that it was out of control. His wife and daughter, Da Mei, and another baby in swaddling clothes had not yet escaped. He shouted anxiously downstairs, but the stairs had broken, making it impossible to get down. Later, he used another ladder to meet them on the street, but they did not come down. Therefore, it is unknown whether they were buried in the fire, dead or alive. Also, Zou's mother, an old woman, was still sick in bed. She jumped out of the window to escape, slightly injured, and was sent to the Yuhe Hospital for treatment. In addition, a yellow dog was burned to death. As for the buildings, the back was the chaff room of the Yifengyuan Teahouse, so the back of the teahouse was also affected. In total, the carpenter's shop, with two rooms and two courtyards, and the upstairs and downstairs buildings were destroyed, and a part of the back of the Yifengyuan Teahouse was also damaged, resulting in a considerable loss. As for the cause of the fire, some said it started in the kitchen downstairs, while others said it was caused by a swallow's nest on the roof. There is no consensus.

Wuxi 86

The Issue of Jurisdiction in Punishing Bandits In the case of punishing bandits, our province has now established temporary command agencies due to the division of areas for bandit suppression. When counties capture bandits, it often involves the issue of jurisdiction in trials. Recently, the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Pacification Commissioner's Office have settled on four measures. The first two measures relate to the punishment of bandits captured by the bandit suppression troops, which are handled directly by the bandit suppression military judge and are not related to the county magistrate. The third measure stipulates that when the county government captures bandits, it should comply with the provincial government's telegram, which is handled by the county government's trial and reported directly to the provincial department for verification. The fourth measure stipulates that cases involving communists should be sent to the Jiangsu Provincial Temporary Military Law Joint Trial Office for interrogation. After receiving the order, County Chief Chen of our county has followed the procedures. For example, Zhou Xinshun, a robber who was executed by shooting a few days ago, was handled in accordance with the provincial government's telegram. As for the communist cases previously solved in Wuxi, such as the Sima Peisheng case, a total of 53 cases have also been submitted to the Yunfa Joint Trial Office a few days ago in accordance with the fourth measure, requesting a review for compliance, and then police officers will be sent to escort the criminals to the province for legal action. False Reporting of Robbery Out of Personal Grudge Tan Weinan, the director of the Twelfth Branch of the Public Security Bureau in the Sixth District (Tianxiashi), received a report from a resident Guo Boxuan of Daixiang on the afternoon of the 11th of this month that a bandit named Dai A Da was knocking on the back door, intending to enter the house to rob, and that he had now been arrested. Director Tan immediately sent patrol officer Zhu Yunjie to accompany Guo Boxuan to take Dai to the bureau. According to Dai A Da's confession, a man named A Gen came to his house that night and invited him to Guo Boxuan's house for a chat. When he arrived at Guo's house, four or five strong men held a rope and tied him up, falsely accusing him of being a thief and arresting him privately, requesting that he be redressed. According to Guo Boxuan and the three arresting officers Zhao Longxing and Shen Jinshi, Dai A Da, the bandit they captured, was the main offender who killed Guo Boxuan's late father, Guo Zizhen. Director Tan, seeing that the confessions of both parties were different, sent bureau member Huang Dexian to investigate Guo's house. According to the long-term worker Wang Xiaofu, Dai A Da had just returned to Wuxi last night, and Boxuan ordered A Gen to invite Dai to his house and then tied him up, claiming that he was robbing and destroying the back door himself. However, the details of the case seem to be a personal grudge. Yesterday, Tan prepared a document and sent both parties to the Public Security Bureau and then to the County Court for trial.

Yixing's Disaster Situation is Extremely Serious, Begging for Aid in Wuxi Sun Gongqi, the county chief of Yixing, stated that more than 700,000 mu of fields in the county were flooded, and there were 200,000 disaster victims who were displaced and had no place to live. The severity of the disaster and the extent of the disaster area are unprecedented. Yesterday, he specially sent a public letter to the local flood relief association, asking for quick allocation of funds to help save the lives of the people.

Nantong 87

The Busy Canal Embezzlement Case is Settled in the Province Li Baoshen, Zhu Ziruo, and Chen Zhongli, key people involved in the Nantong Busy Canal Embezzlement Case, were sent to the province by the county government. The Finance Department has now handed them over to the guard for supervision. At the same time, the original tax collectors were urged to come to the department to check the facts. After Tian Tiesen, the director of land tax, was sent to the province, he has been sent to the Zhenjiang County Government for supervision, and his son, Liu Dacong, the chief of the levy, has been ordered to hand over the funds.

Zhenjiang 88

The Emergency Relief Association Ordered the Salvage of Floating Corpses The Jiangsu Provincial Flood Emergency Relief Association yesterday sent a telegram to the county chiefs of Zhenjiang and Jiangbei, stating that the Fish Telegram from the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association's office in Yangzhou had been received, stating that the disaster victims from various places reported that the dead bodies in the river were floating around indefinitely, requesting measures to be taken to salvage them to prevent epidemics. Our office is now urgently saving lives and is busy with work and cannot take care of everything. Therefore, we specially send this telegram to you, asking you to send telegrams to the county chiefs in each disaster area to take measures to salvage and bury the corpses, in order to prevent epidemics. You should follow the instructions.

Gaoyou 89

A Record of the Gaoyou Relief Situation Details of the flood disaster in Gaoyou have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that there are currently three relief agencies in the area: (1) The Shanghai Hua Yang Yizhen Association's office in Gaoyou, located in Wanfeng Sauce Garden in the South Gate. According to Mr. Wang, the owner of the store, the Shanghai Hua Yang Yizhen Association sent German missionary Ke Weilian (transliteration) to Gaoyou on the 8th to establish the office in Gaoyou. Mr. Ke telegraphed the General Association on the 9th, requesting that 6,000 yuan be remitted to Gaoyou for distribution. Mr. Ke went to Xinghua last night to investigate the disaster situation. (2) The Shanghai China Jisheng Association's office in Gaoyou, located in Wanhe Lu Chenhang. According to Mr. Yin Shunzhang, an official of the office, the Shanghai General Association sent one person in charge, Zhang Jixian, and seven staff members to Gaoyou for relief. They have now transported 3,000 bags of flour and 200 bags of rice, but the distribution has been temporarily suspended due to the lack of specific measures. Commissioner Zhang went to Shanghai on the 9th to report on the disaster situation. (3) The Jiangsu Flood Relief Association's office in Gaoyou is temporarily working on a boat near the Pipa Gate. According to Mr. Zhu Qilu, the person in charge of relief affairs who came to Gaoyou, the General Association not only sent me to Gaoyou for relief, but also sent 12 staff members to assist. He personally brought 10,000 yuan in relief funds with him. This morning (the 10th), he sent a boat to Zhenjiang to load 150 bags of rice first. The rest of the relief supplies will be requested successively in the future due to the lack of accurate numbers. Regarding rescue, the Gaoyou Flood Temporary Relief Association has been requested to hire 40 private boats to go to various villages for rescue, rescuing about 1,000 refugees every day. After the rescue, they are temporarily sent to the reception center. Those who volunteer to go south are sent separately. Regarding reception, there is now a reception center in Dawang Temple, which is the responsibility of Mr. Zhao Huchen. It receives about 4,000 refugees every day. Some stay for one night and are sent south, while others who do not want to go elsewhere are given two meals a day. The order is good. There is also a reception center in Yongxing Temple in Jieshou, which receives more than 400 refugees every day.

Letter

Letter from the Representatives of the Disaster Victims in Suining County 90

Shanghai Shenbao Hall, respected: The flood disaster in Suining is extremely serious, with no autumn harvest at all. The disaster victims are all over the fields, and the dangerous situation is everywhere. We have telegraphed to the authorities at all levels and various charitable organizations, appealing for relief. Unexpectedly, on September 1, there was another continuous rainfall, day and night. The floodwater in the fields was more than ten feet deep, not only submerging the replanted buckwheat and vegetables, but also washing away people, livestock, and houses. Such a terrible disaster is unprecedented. The disaster victims are in dire need of rescue. In addition to sending telegrams, please send someone to investigate and provide relief, so as to avoid the danger of chaos in the country. We are very anxious and await your orders. Respectfully, the representatives of the disaster victims in Suining County, Zhang Ziyun, Xu Shaoping, Wang Huaju, Zhuo Zaiqing, Liu Ludong, Yuan Xianzhi, and Yuan Xingcun.

Letter from the Gaoyou County Flood Relief Association 91

Dear Sir/Madam: We were shocked to read the special telegram from Zhenjiang on the 3rd in your newspaper's "Domestic Important News" column on September 4, which stated that the number of disaster victims in each county was about 30,000 in Gaoyou and Lishui. The flood disaster in Gaoyou is the most serious in Jiangnan, with 195 breaches and about 160,000 disaster victims. We have repeatedly telegraphed abroad for relief and reported to the province, all stating that there are more than 100,000 disaster victims. The statement that there are 30,000 disaster victims in Gaoyou is definitely not true. Please correct it. This is very important. Gaoyou County Flood Relief Association, September 9

Women's 50-meter Race Re-run This Afternoon at 2 PM 103

In the women's 50-meter final the day before yesterday, apart from Zhang Pingxian who clearly reached the finish line first, the remaining four were very close when crossing the finish line, making it difficult to see clearly at the time, which led to questions about the results. The finish line judges discussed it once the night before, but without result. It was not until yesterday morning that the head judge decided that there was no problem with Zhang Pingxian being first. The four ladies who crossed the line together, Si Tuwei, Li Baohui, Xue Qiding and Ma Yufang will re-run the final today at 2 PM to determine the positions for second, third and fourth, in order to be fair. The organizing committee notified all the athletes yesterday, fearing they might not arrive by this morning. We hope that the four ladies will be on site promptly at 2 PM this afternoon to await the re-run final.

Fudan Team Wins Men's Volleyball Championship in the Final 104

Straight Three Wins Over Daxia

The two volleyball powerhouses on the sea, Fudan and Daxia Universities, competed at the Longpo Race Road field yesterday afternoon, with a large crowd of men and women watching. Fudan showed their best skills and defeated Daxia straight in three sets to win the championship.

Set No. Result of First Half Winner

Set 1 11 to 6 21 to 13 Fudan Wins Daxia

Set 2 11 to 5 21 to 10 Fudan Wins Daxia

Set 3 11 to 6 21 to 12 Fudan Wins Daxia

▲ Fudan Team Shows Great Power From yesterday's match, it is clear how the situation was from the scores. It was far from the fierce and close match that was hoped for. Daxia was not Fudan's opponent at all. In the first set, Fudan won the first half 11 to 6 and won the first set 21 to 13. In the second set, Daxia was still not in good form, and Fudan again won first 11 to 5, ending 21 to 10. In the third set, Daxia once led 5 to 4, but after one point, the situation changed again, 11 to 6, and the set ended 21 to 12. As a result, the score was 3 to 0.

▲ General Fei's Reputation is Well-Deserved Fudan's performance yesterday was much better than the day before, with a hundred times more momentum. Whether it was cooperation or smashing, everything was perfect. General Fei, Cao Zan, showed his amazing skills, striking without mercy. The balls that went out of bounds the day before were all within the lines yesterday. Daxia was like being under artillery fire for three sets.

▲ Chen Baoqiu Plays Sick There are reasons why Daxia was inferior. Their main player, Chen Baoqiu, participated in the match while sick, with a white cloth tied tightly around his head. His decisive smash that used to determine the outcome was rarely seen yesterday, only two or three times in total. He had to switch to a winger in the third set, and defender Wei Dingyi's smashes were mostly unsuccessful, so they lost.

Wang Jihuai Creates New National Record in Pentathlon 114

In the drizzling rain, the pentathlon competition began. There were few spectators outside the field, and there were more referees in the field than athletes. Therefore, compared with the previous day, the track and field had a feeling of past and present. Fortunately, the athletes who came to the field were all energetic and wanted to show their skills.

Pentathlon 115

The pentathlon is a special event for Shanghai athletes. At last year's National Games, held in Hangzhou, the first and second places in the pentathlon were all won by Shanghai. Therefore, yesterday's pentathlon competition was expected to have good results. However, after the news that Wang Jihuai had injured his ribs in the long jump the day before yesterday, those who were enthusiastic about this event were unhappy and sighed that the pentathlon competition would be inferior because of it. Unexpectedly, to everyone's delight, when the reporter arrived at the field at about 1 PM yesterday afternoon, Wang Jihuai had already arrived before me. The reporter was deeply afraid of psychological effects, so he only encouraged him and did not mention any foot tendon sprains. The result of the competition was very satisfactory, and he actually created a new national record with a score of 2821.305 points, exceeding Chen Shengkui's score in the North China Games by more than 268 points. Yesterday's competition also involved the 10,000 meters, which reversed the order. After running the 200 meters, they ran the 1,500 meters without resting for even a quarter of an hour, so the results were slightly inferior. Otherwise, the total score would have been even more impressive. Hao Chunde, the pentathlon champion of last year's National Games, was inferior in the 1,500 meters and javelin, so he was ranked second. The complete scores of each person are recorded below.

Decathlon 116

Luo Chuanxian and Zhong Lianji Compete for the Championship

Cao Yu, the decathlon champion of last year's National Games, was injured in the back of his thigh due to excessive practice during the summer vacation. After two weeks of rest, he had fully recovered. Unexpectedly, his old injury recurred during the pole vault the day before yesterday, so he gave up yesterday's decathlon and pole vault. Therefore, yesterday's decathlon competition was not very exciting. Initially, there were seven participants. After the 100 meters and long jump, Li Lin and Jiang Shanjing also gave up halfway. Therefore, only Zhong Lianji, Luo Chuanxian, Liang Tiancheng, Liu Menglin, and Li Guowei completed the first half. Judging from the scores of the first five events, Zhong had a total of 2773.81 points, and seemed to have a better chance of winning the championship. However, Zhong's performance in the last five events was not as good as in the first five events. Luo Chuanxian may have a chance to catch up, because Luo can beat Zhong by a lot in the high hurdles, discus, and javelin. According to the reporter's speculation, the 1,500 meters is the focus of the competition between Zhong and Luo for the decathlon championship. Liang Tiancheng has a third hope, and Li Guowei's scores are too far apart, so he may be eliminated. What will happen? Let's listen to the analysis today. The scores of the first half of the decathlon are recorded below.

Wen Jingduo Breaks National Record in 100-meter Backstroke on First Day of Men's and Women's Swimming 119

Time: 1 minute 36.7 seconds

At 7 PM last night, the city's best male and female swimmers gathered at the Jiaotong University swimming pool in Xujiahui, each showing their best skills and competing against each other, causing 600-700 spectators to watch from the sidelines, cheering and applauding thunderously. The new national record for the 100-meter backstroke was created by Wen Jingduo in this tense atmosphere. The progress of each event is briefly described below:

(1) General Comments on the Competition 120

▲ In the second group of the men's 50-meter freestyle, Lin Jiangshui's swimming posture was quite good. He was ranked second when he reached the finish line, but unfortunately, he swam out of his lane carelessly and was disqualified.

▲ Gong Xiji, who won the first place in the women's 50-meter freestyle, was tall and sturdy, with a masculine appearance. Her swimming posture was very graceful.

▲ The first place winners of the first and second groups in the men's 100-meter backstroke preliminary both used the method of stroking both arms backward at the same time, while the second place winners of the two groups both used the method of stroking one arm backward alternately. The spectators were all surprised. Yu Binqi, a backstroke expert, was disqualified for crossing the line while swimming. Otherwise, Yu would have won the second place and would have been promising in tomorrow's final.

▲ In the first group of the 1,500-meter preliminary, the first, second, and third places were about 50 meters apart, reaching the finish line in order, which was very interesting. In the second group, Chen Quantai had already swum 36 laps and was in second place, but suddenly had a stomachache, so he had to give up the competition, which was a pity.

▲ In the first group of the 200-meter breaststroke preliminary, Su Zuqing cramped in the pool when he was swimming enthusiastically, rising and falling. Other athletes by the pool saw the danger and bravely jumped into the pool in groups of three or five to rescue him. All the spectators applauded and celebrated.

▲ The competition in the second group of the men's 100-meter freestyle was extremely fierce. Yin Yanjun, the first place winner, and Chen Xiannan, the second place winner, were only inches apart when they reached the finish line.

▲ There was only one lady, Gong Xiji, in the women's 100-meter freestyle. The three Chen sisters were temporarily invited to join the performance. Ms. Chen Baoxuan, the oldest at 13 years old, led first when she swam to 25 meters, but was soon overtaken by Ms. Gong, resulting in second place. Ms. Chen Baodang, who was slightly younger than her sister, was also able to complete the entire course, which was quite difficult. The youngest, Ms. Chen Baolian, was only 9 years old, petite and exquisite, lively and extraordinary, with a graceful posture, and will definitely become a swimming expert in the future. The reporter can predict.

Ten Thousand Meter Final: Ma Fengrui Takes First Place 123

In the ten thousand meter run, judging by yesterday's final, one could say that talent was abundant. Thirty-one people started, and more than twenty finished the race. The distance between the top six was quite close. The intense competition was unprecedented in Shanghai's ten thousand meter races. Wang Zhenglin followed Ma Fengrui right from the start. For seven or eight laps, it was like a good car towing a broken car, lap after lap, a comical sight. After ten laps, Wang was no match for Ma, gradually falling behind, becoming out of reach, ending up twenty to thirty meters behind Ma. Xu Yanbo, Chen Xingpei, Dong Jiaxie, and Chen Luzhou, each panting like an ox, followed closely behind. In this situation, it was truly uncertain who would win. In the end, Ma was indeed Ma. When this "Ma" was mentioned, everyone looked up to his head and bowed at his hooves. Wang Zhenglin, Xu Yanbo, and Chen Xingpei fought to the very end, securing second, third, and fourth places, respectively. Chen Xuzhou is old and, as learned, had been ill for a long time, resulting in a decline in energy, which led to his failure to place. The other competitors were in good spirits. Few dropped out midway and failed to finish the entire course, which is truly a memorable event. Furthermore, not many were absent during the roll call, which shows the interest of the city's residents in long-distance running. However, observing all the competitors, many had poor form, taking steps that were too high and employing a jumping posture, which is a major flaw in long-distance running and should be improved in the future. The results of the ten thousand meter race are recorded below:

First Place: Ma Fengrui

Second Place: Wang Zhenglin

Third Place: Xu Yanbo

Fourth Place: Chen Xingpei

Time: 37 minutes, 16 and 5/5 seconds.

National Arts Judge Tong Zhongyi 125

Mr. Tong Zhongyi served as the head judge for the national martial arts competition today. In the twenty-eighth year of the Guangxu Emperor's reign, he worked as a bodyguard in Fengtian. In the thirtieth year, he was an officer in the Fengtian Forward Army Patrol Team. In the thirty-second year, he returned to his hometown. In the second year of the Xuantong Emperor's reign, he served as the chief martial arts instructor of the Third Regiment of the Imperial Guards. In the first year of the Republic, he served as an orthopedic doctor in the First Regiment of the Chahar Banner Army. In the sixth year, he returned to serve as the chief martial arts and wrestling instructor of the Third Battalion, Sixth Regiment, Fifth Route Army of Anhui. In the seventh year, he served as the chief martial arts and wrestling instructor of the First Battalion, Second Regiment, Mixed Brigade of the Four Provinces Police Affairs Envoy's Guard. In the ninth year, he served as the company commander of the Third Company of the First Battalion. In the thirteenth year, he served as the captain of the Wuqiao Security Regiment. In the sixteenth year, he again served as the chief martial arts and wrestling instructor of the Zhili Army Cadre School. In the seventeenth year, he came to Shanghai and served as the director of academic affairs of the Guo Yu Martial Arts Research Association, and also served as the director of academic affairs of the Shaolin branch of the Shanghai National Martial Arts Hall. In the seventeenth year, he participated in the national examination and received a certificate of excellence. He also served as a supervisor of the Hangzhou National Martial Arts and Games Meeting and as a judge of the Shanghai National Martial Arts Competition.

Nine Advertising Boards Set Up 132

To attract the attention of the citizens of Beijing, the Organizing Committee has set up nine particularly large advertising boards at Xinjiekou, Gulou, Confucius Temple, Xiaguan Railway Station, and other locations. The number of events, participating units, and types of championships are clearly displayed. The sides of the advertising boards are painted with colorful designs, which are extremely beautiful.

Temporary Post Office Established in Beijing 133

The National Games will be held in Beijing on National Day. However, during the meeting period, there will be a large number of letters exchanged between the organizing committee and various parties, and the number of letters exchanged by the athletes and staff from various provinces will also be very large. To facilitate postal operations, the Directorate General of Posts will establish a temporary post office near the venue of the National Games before National Day so that all letters sent and received by the staff and athletes of the National Games are concentrated in one place. Letters sent from this office will be stamped with a commemorative National Games mark for souvenirs. The Directorate General of Posts has submitted this matter to the Ministry of Communications for approval. As soon as the instructions are received, the Directorate General of Posts will begin preparations.

Local News

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram Calling for Peace 134

The Whole Country Joins Forces to Relieve Disaster

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram yesterday, which said, "To the Nanjing National Government: Amidst the atmosphere of silence, ominous news is spreading at home and abroad, claiming that the situation in Hunan is tense. We are shocked to hear this. Ever since the initial dispute in Guangdong this year, our Chamber has sent telegrams calling for national wealth to be devoted to large-scale disaster relief and national forces to be devoted to large-scale bandit suppression. If war breaks out again, financial and military resources will be unable to handle both, and we will only be able to watch as our country falls into the hands of bandits and our people become starving refugees. Furthermore, under the rule of the party, all disputes should be properly handled in accordance with the party's constitution. If we resort to war, it would be self-destructive to the life of the party's rule and the life of the Chinese nation. Since then, although the dispute has not been properly resolved, the Guangdong side has repeatedly made informal declarations that it will not hinder the military operations of bandit suppression, even if it goes against public opinion. Therefore, for several months, the troops have not moved a single step beyond the Five Ridges. The people of the country believe that the Guangdong side also deeply understands the power of public opinion and the need to protect the lifeline of the nation, so there is a glimmer of hope for a peaceful future. Moreover, it is increasingly clear that the crux of the dispute is not that there is no way to resolve it except through military force. The previous storms and tense atmosphere were caused by those with ulterior motives who stirred up trouble, not the original intention. Unexpectedly, man-made disasters and natural disasters have come together. The military operation of bandit suppression has just begun to succeed, but floods have caused disasters in as many as seventeen provinces across the country. According to estimates, the number of people affected by the disaster is about fifty to sixty million, almost one-seventh of our country's total population. The tragedy is even worse than the great famine in the northwest last year. Moreover, the areas affected by this disaster are mostly in the areas of the country known as the financial and tax areas. The treasures have been swept away by the waves, and the situation is different from that of drought. Even if the entire country, from top to bottom, exhausts all its resources and makes a concerted effort to provide disaster relief, it is still feared that the disaster area is too large and the resources are too weak to raise the disaster-stricken people from the ravines. Therefore, the news of this disaster has spread, and donations have poured in from home and abroad, because it is a human constant to love life and hate killing. Our country's unprecedented disaster is enough to arouse their compassion and sympathy. As the saying goes, 'When the people are in mourning, crawl to save them.' At this time, more than half of the country's territory is in a disaster area, which is the day to crawl to save the mourning, not the time to compete for pride. According to the meaning of the Spring and Autumn Annals, war is a major taboo for mourning, because it takes advantage of people's danger for one's own benefit. How can we take advantage of the day when people across the country are starving to death to achieve our own goals? Wherever the army goes, the expenses are huge. In a melee, there is no way to have both. It is bound to rob everything to fill the military needs. It is expected that the day when the soldiers at the front come into contact will be the time when national relief is suspended, and tens of millions of disaster victims will die. The officials in power must have a heart of benevolence and will not bear to trap the people of the country in the realm of destruction due to a single mistake. Previously, I read Commander-in-Chief Chiang's letter to the people of the country and Deputy Commander Zhang's telegram, which also stated that the country's steps are difficult and the people's livelihood is haggard, and it is urgent to recuperate and rejuvenate, and there is no room for war again. Benevolent words and good news are admired by the whole world. I hope that the gentlemen will lay down their weapons and find other ways to deal with the aftermath, and keep in mind the warnings of danger and perish and do not fall into the criticism of leading the war. Not only can the disaster victims rely on it to entrust their lives, but the continuation of the national foundation lies in this. Sincerely calling out, I hope you will understand." Shanghai Chamber of Commerce bows.

Shanghai Business Community to Launch Peace and Disaster Relief Association 135

Li Shizeng's Reply Telegram Agrees

Li Shizeng replied yesterday to Zhang Gongquan, Lin Kanghou, Ye Zhuotang, and others in a telegram, which said, "(Translated) To Mr. Lin Kanghou and Mr. Ye Zhuotang of the Shanghai Bankers' Association: I have just replied to Brother Zhang Gongquan in a telegram as follows: To Mr. Zhang Gongquan: I have received your letter. Our views on peace and disaster relief are the same. Recently, all sectors of Beijing have launched a Peace and Disaster Relief Association. I hope that you, Mr. Lin, and the comrades of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Bankers' Association will also proceed in a consistent manner as stated in your letter and in the spirit of the past peace movement to promote the early realization of peace. The people's livelihood of the whole country will really depend on it. Yuying bows. I also pray that you will all agree with this view. Yuying bows." After receiving the telegram, Zhang, Lin, Ye, and others held a meeting with Wang Xiaolai, the chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and others, and decided to convene a meeting in the next few days to advocate peace and request the Guangdong region to cease military operations.

Boy Scout Fundraising Completed Yesterday 136

Totaling More Than Ten Thousand Yuan

The results of the Shanghai Boy Scout fundraising were announced yesterday at the Moore Memorial Church. Representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, and the Municipal Education Bureau, as well as the entire staff of the East Asia Boy Scouts, were present to supervise. From 9:00 AM to 7:00 PM, the work of sorting and auditing was completed. A total of more than ten thousand yuan was raised, which was still far from the association's original ideal, but the enthusiasm of the city's Boy Scouts was admirable. The results of yesterday's opening of the collection boxes were as follows: 2,199.3 yuan in silver dollars, 22,327.5 cents in small silver coins, and 59,585 copper coins. Combined with the results from the previous day, the total was 5,599.3 yuan in silver dollars, 52,329.5 cents in small silver coins, and 129,168 copper coins. After deducting 14.1 yuan in counterfeit silver dollars, 1487 cents in inferior coins, and 244.8 yuan for the printing of bamboo collection boxes and other expenses (all meal expenses, transportation expenses, and other expenses were borne by the Municipal Council), the net amount was 5,340.4 yuan in silver dollars, 50,842.5 cents in small silver coins, and 129,168 copper coins. The above amounts were certified to be correct by Zhu Jiarang, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Wu Lai, the representative of the Municipal Government, and Wu Zengfu, the representative of the Municipal Education Bureau. They were immediately handed over to the Shanghai All-Provinces Flood Disaster Relief Association, which issued receipts for storage, transfer, and distribution to benefit the disaster victims.

Disaster Relief News from Various Provinces Yesterday 137

Disaster Victims Begin to Gather for Shelter

Yesterday was the first day that the Shanghai Disaster Relief Office concentrated the disaster victims who came to Shanghai from various places at the first shelter on Liuying Road, Zhabei. The details are recorded below:

▲Transportation in Batches: After the staff members of the office gathered at the office yesterday morning, they set off separately. The China Moving Company allocated four cars for transportation. The north and south were far apart, and it took time to travel back and forth. The cars made fifteen trips in the morning to transport the disaster victims from the Chaozhou Wuyi Villa. In the afternoon, they transported the disaster victims from the Yongxi Hall Zhejiang Shaoxing Association. If time allowed, the disaster victims from the Qu Zhenren Temple would also be transported together. However, the disaster victims from the Chao Hui Villa would have to be transported today.

▲Equipment Inside the Shelter: Yesterday the weather was uncertain due to rain, so the Kangding reorganization plan of the office could not be implemented. Only the number of disaster victims was counted according to the points. If it was confirmed that a family had twelve or thirteen members, they would live in one room. Approximately ten to twelve people lived in each room. Each room was 25 feet long and 10 feet wide. The beds were paved with 2-inch thick wooden boards, more than 2 feet above the ground, with shelves placed on top and coal ash paved underneath. There were paths made of mud bricks, and there were corridors along the corridors with benches. When the disaster victims from Chaozhou Wuyi Villa first moved in, although they had been informed in advance, many disaster victims were still doubtful, and some even cried and refused to get in the car. After the staff persuaded them, they followed them. When they arrived at the shelter, they were all overjoyed to see where they lived, and some even cried for joy. However, the shelter had not yet distributed the clothing for the disaster victims to use at this time.

▲Injections and Vaccinations: All disaster victims transported to the first shelter on Liuying Road by car must first be injected with a vaccination and vaccinated against smallpox by the technicians sent by the health team of the office. Then, the staff of the office could assign them housing, lead them inside, and immediately provide them with food. Each meal consisted of one vegetarian dish and one soup, which was very clean. The dishes eaten by the staff members were also the same as those of the disaster victims. It was also learned that after all the disaster victims were concentrated, barbers would be hired to the shelter to shave their long hair in batches and have them take a bath to maintain cleanliness.

▲Telegram Not to Send More: The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs received a telegram from the Hubei Civil Affairs Department yesterday, stating that 20,000 disaster victims would be transported to Shanghai in batches and asked if they could be accommodated. The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs responded that there were already many disaster victims coming to Shanghai from various provinces, the supplies were huge, and the equipment was not easy to obtain, so they telegraphed the Hubei Civil Affairs Department not to transport disaster victims to Shanghai.

Yesterday, Cantonese Compatriots from the Hankou Disaster Area Arrived in Shanghai 138

The Shanghai Guangzhao Association and the Cantonese Overseas Chinese Business Federation had previously purchased a large amount of grain and medicine to send people to Hankou for emergency relief due to the severe flood disaster in Hankou. Yesterday morning, the Huangpu steamship carried the first batch of 78 Cantonese compatriots, men, women, and children, from the Hankou disaster area. When they arrived at the pier, the directors of the association, Chen Bingqian, together with the staff, personally supervised the care and sent them to the predetermined Mingli Guangtailai Hotel for accommodation. In the afternoon, they took Dr. Huang Wen and others to the hotel to give injections for dysentery. They will be sent back to their hometowns another day.

Emergency Relief Association Held an Extraordinary Meeting Yesterday 139

The Shanghai Fundraising Association for Emergency Relief of Flood Disasters in Various Provinces held an extraordinary standing committee meeting yesterday at 3:00 PM. Xu Shiying, Wang Yiting, Zhu Qinglan, Zhang Xiaolin, Xiang Songmao, and Li Zuyu attended. Xu Shiying chaired the meeting. (A) Reporting Items: 1. From the 2nd to the 12th of this month, the association received a total of silver taels 5,874.42 yuan less than was already on hand, with a balance of 200 silver ingots, a balance of 72 yuan in subsidiary silver coins, and new receipts of 394,580.055 yuan (donations received on behalf of others from September 8 to September 12 are not included), 185 silver ingots, 55 yuan in miscellaneous paper money, 20 yuan in counterfeit paper money, 5 yuan in changed paper money, and 9 yuan in subsidiary silver coins. Of this, 50,000 yuan was allocated from the four banks to Hubei and Jiangsu (15,000 yuan each), Anhui and Hunan (8,000 yuan each), and Zhejiang (4,000 yuan). The actual balance was 338,706.13 yuan, 385 silver ingots, 55 yuan in miscellaneous paper money, 20 yuan in counterfeit paper money, 5 yuan in changed paper money, and 81 yuan in subsidiary silver coins. 2. Report on relief supplies received. 3. From the 8th to the 13th, a total of 192 documents and telegrams were received. 4. From the 8th to the 13th, a total of 158 documents and telegrams were sent. 5. A total of 28 documents and telegrams were received from various provinces and counties reporting disasters and asking for relief. (B) Proposals: 1. A resolution was passed to allocate 90,000 yuan for relief in Jiangsu (10,000 yuan each for Jiangning and the capital), 50,000 yuan in Hunan, 90,000 yuan in Anhui, 60 bags of red sorghum from Anhui, 50,000 yuan in Henan, 30,000 yuan in Zhejiang, 20,000 yuan in Shaanxi, and 20,000 yuan in Gansu. 2. A proposal to check the relief lists and receipt stubs and to compare the newspaper advertisements with the receipt stubs was decided to be handled by the audit team. Wen Lanting reported that the decision was followed. 3. A proposal from Committee Member Li Zuyu for uniform fundraising methods was submitted to the joint meeting on Thursday for discussion. 4. A letter from Long Xiangyun, delivered by Standing Committee Member Wang Xiaozhong, questioned whether the printing expenses were too high and whether there was any embezzlement, requesting a thorough investigation and report. It was decided to hand it over to the audit team for thorough investigation and report. 5. The General Affairs Team proposed whether the advertising expenses should be treated as legitimate expenses in accordance with the regulations of the Relief Association. It was decided to treat them as legitimate expenses in accordance with the Relief Association's precedent, and Wen Lanting was entrusted to negotiate discounts with various newspapers. 6. The General Affairs Team proposed whether the remittance fees, transportation fees, postage fees, and all local expenses of the relief workers could be treated as legitimate expenses under the relief funds. It was resolved that it should be handled in accordance with the Relief Committee's travel expense regulations and treated as legitimate expenses. 7. Should a telegram be sent to all relief workers to request local officials and gentry to establish pawnshops for cattle? It was resolved to do so and the telegram was sent immediately. 8. Jia Ruxiong wrote to say that the disaster area was vast and asked whether a relief copper coin could be added to the price of streetcar and public bus tickets. This was rejected.

News from the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association 140

▲Progress Report: Since its establishment on the 18th of last month, the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association has been working with extraordinary intensity. All trivial news has been published daily. Now, in order to allow philanthropists to understand the association's progress, we have specially copied a letter from the association to the Provincial Relief Committee and present it below. Respectfully, the province of Jiangsu is unfortunate, with floods raging. Over fifty counties have reported disasters, and the most and second-most severely affected number nearly thirty. The disaster area is vast, unprecedented in history. Our colleagues are heartbroken and alarmed. We have undertaken the task entrusted by the general assembly to organize the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association to engage in relief efforts. We are also grateful for the allocation of one million yuan in public bonds as security, which will be managed together. This demonstrates the utmost concern for the disaster-stricken people, and we are filled with admiration. It is understood that official relief and charitable relief share the same ultimate goal. When people are drowning and starving, how dare we lag behind? At the beginning of our planning, we took the division of disaster areas and on-site surveys as our starting point. We divided the areas into the Ningxu area, led by Commissioner Qiao Baoyuan; the Yangzhen area, led by Commissioner Yuan Jimei; and the Zhunyang area, led by Commissioner Zhu Qiliu and Commissioner Chen Huichen. We also printed survey forms to be filled out separately. We also compiled a general organizational outline and two detailed rules for handling affairs and distributing aid, as our relief guidelines. After deliberation, a basic framework has been established. In the midst of these preparations, news came of the breach of the Gao-Shao Canal, causing immense suffering. Jing Sheng, having been mistakenly elected by his colleagues, brought cash and dry rations, and rushed to Zhen overnight. He met with Mr. Leng, Mr. Lu, Mr. Hu, Mr. Wang, and other gentlemen, as well as gentlemen from the general assembly, at the Chamber of Commerce to discuss emergency relief methods. A provincial office was immediately established in cooperation with the Jiangbei Flood Relief Association. Several steamships and civilian boats were dispatched in teams to provide assistance. Chairman Ye was also accompanied to the Gao-Shao-Baoying area for on-site surveys. The sight of the dead drifting and the living crying for help was heartbreaking. Consequently, offices were established in various counties and towns along the canal, including Yangzhou, Gaoyou, Sisui, Baoying, and Xinghua, with the primary task of establishing shelters to provide settlement for the survivors of this catastrophe. Currently, six shelters have been established in Yangzhou, three in Zhenjiang, four in Gaoyou, one in Jieshou, one in Sisui, and two in Baoying, accommodating over 20,000 people. However, some of these people have moved on to relatives and friends. If we include the number of people who have been transported, the total is estimated to be between 40,000 and 50,000. The rules for the offices and shelters, as well as the transportation methods, have been carefully established amidst busy schedules. We have been tirelessly planning and working day and night. After completing the survey and returning to Shanghai, we received a letter assigning the emergency relief of twenty-two counties, including Pixiao, to our association, along with the entire province's winter relief for this year. After reading this, our colleagues felt that with the area divided and the scope smaller, both personnel and funds would be easier to manage. This arrangement aligns with our initial intentions. However, the counties assigned this time, such as Gaoyou, Jiangdu, Xinghua, Baoying, Jiangpu, Gangshan, Funing, Huaian, and Huaiyin, are all the most severely affected areas. In addition to the undammed breach of the Gao-Shao Canal, the counties in the lower reaches of the river are still completely flooded. People are displaced, and there is no intact land. The suffering is unprecedented in human history and rarely seen in a century. We pace around the room, our minds exhausted. We have already hired experienced and reputable individuals who have been involved in relief work for many years to serve as directors of investigations and distributions in each county. We have also allocated funds from the general assembly to be transferred to them for investigations and distributions. If there are insufficient funds for any county, we will use charitable relief as a backup. In terms of investigation and distribution procedures, in addition to the offices managing shelters and porridge kitchens, and hiring boats and purchasing relief supplies, which can only be calculated based on receipts, for provincial funds, we still intend to uniformly use relief vouchers. This is to emphasize the seriousness of relief funds amidst the urgency of emergency relief. (Abbreviated below)

▲Telegraphic Excerpts: The association has been receiving dozens of telegrams daily from various parties regarding relief efforts, etc. We have selected a few telegrams below. Governor Zhang's telegram to Jiang: "Respectfully reading your telegram, I am deeply honored. I, Jiang, as the Director of Pacification, am responsible for comforting the people. Witnessing the suffering, I feel deeply indebted. Your concern for the hungry and drowning, and your enthusiasm for saving the world, have inspired all who hear of it. Although I am unworthy, I will follow in your footsteps and do my best to assist in saving these disaster-stricken people." Also, Commissioner Chen Huichen's telegram from the Baoying Office: "The Jiangbei Emergency Relief Association has received 500 bags of flour. Director Hu of the Civil Affairs Department visited Bao and surveyed the disaster on the first day of the new year, deeming it extremely severe. He also inspected two shelters." Also, Director Hu of Zhenjiang's telegram to Commissioner Wang Yiting: "A meeting is scheduled to be held on [date]. Please come with Commissioner Cheng. I heard that Commissioner Wang is busy with relief efforts and will only be able to attend the meeting in Zhen on [date]."

Work of the China International Famine Relief Commission in Disaster Relief 141

▲Yangzhou Branch Begins Distribution: The association received a letter from the Yangzhou branch reporting the following: (1) The main relief item is flour. Please have the headquarters in Shanghai purchase it. (1) The main relief item is flour. Please have the headquarters in Shanghai purchase it. (2) The distribution team has already departed, focusing on poor and remote areas that have been overlooked by various charitable groups. (3) The upper, middle, and lower reaches of the three rivers have all suffered catastrophic damage. There are over 1.1 million disaster victims, half of whom are extremely poor. With winter approaching, please prepare more cotton clothes and pants.

▲Flour and Old Clothes Transported to Yangzhou: After receiving the above report, the association has purchased 10,000 bags of flour, with 5,000 bags being loaded onto the Datong Steamer today and another 5,000 bags to be loaded tomorrow. The association has also transported several hundred pieces of used clothing to the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce for transfer to Yangzhou.

▲Establishment of the Xinghua Branch: The Xinghua branch of the China International Famine Relief Commission has been officially established. Reverend Ke Weilian is the Western president, and Commissioner Hua Zhen is the Chinese president. The members are Hong Yixin, Yan Lunan, Gu Zifang, Zhu Liangfu, Xi Dingjue, Rong Yuzhi, Wu Xinhua, etc., who have divided into groups to carry out their work.

▲Hu Wenhu Donates More Wan Jin You: Mr. Hu Wenhu, owner of the Tiger Balm Yong An Tang in Singapore, is enthusiastic about philanthropy. He has repeatedly donated large sums of money and medicines. Yesterday, he telegraphed the association, donating another 26 boxes of Wan Jin You. A philanthropist like Mr. Hu is worthy of admiration.

▲Hangzhou Used Clothing and Bedding Relief Association: As the weather is getting colder, the disaster victims are suffering from both hunger and cold. In addition to food, there is an urgent need for clothing and bedding. Philanthropists in Hangzhou have organized the Used Clothing and Bedding Relief Association to donate used clothing and bedding to benefit the disaster victims. Yesterday, 453 items were sent to the association, which plans to transport them to the disaster area for distribution as soon as possible.

▲Chen Fang's Photo Frame Stall Raises Funds: Chen Fang, the owner of the Chen Fang photo frame stall at Dongxin Bridge on Avenue Edward VII, considering the severity of the floods in various places, believes that even as a small business owner, he should do what he can to help those in need. He has enthusiastically solicited donations from nearby vendors, etc. In addition to Chen Fang's own donation of five yuan, some donated two yuan, some donated one yuan, and many donated two jiao. A total of 78 households donated 37.5 yuan in silver dollars and 68 jiao in small coins. This was delivered to the China International Famine Relief Commission yesterday for forwarding to the disaster area. A small business owner with such enthusiasm is truly admirable.

▲Dongtai Welcomes the Transport Team to Open the Seaport: The Dongtai Association in Shanghai recently received a report from Dongtai stating that the Yanken Company is obstructing the drainage of water. It states that the Dafeng and Yuhua Companies are located downstream of the Caozhen Gate diversion canal, near the end of the Doulong Port. Before the company was established, it was all Cao marshland. In the past, when the Huai River flooded, the dikes of the Yun Canal were opened to release water into the sea, but not all of it was discharged through the Doulong Port. Because of the nearby Cao marshland, there were branch rivers and small ports above, which diverted water into the sea. Since the establishment of the company, it has built high dikes inside and outside the reclamation area, preventing the drainage of water from the nine counties in the lower reaches of the river. During the great flood, the counties observed this situation, and the provincial councilors of Taizhou requested the opening of the dikes, which was approved. This summer, with continuous rain for weeks, there was no way to drain the water. The local people also believed that the dams of Dafeng and Yuhua were obstructing the flow. This was recognized by representatives from various counties and approved by the Second Jiangsu Provincial Representative Conference. The provincial government ordered the Dongtai County to supervise the opening of the company's seaports. In late August, the county dispatched the director of the Public Security Bureau to open the Nan Zhong and Liang Mao You Rivers first. Unexpectedly, the company re-blocked the mouths of the various Mao You Rivers shortly after the opening personnel left. Their intention is not only to disregard the provincial orders but also to trap the people of the nine counties in the lower reaches of the river to death. A telegram has been received from the provincial government requesting Pacification Commissioner Zhang and Security Director Li Chuliang to send a team to Dongtai to open the seaports of various companies. The people are extremely grateful, believing that the accumulated water can quickly enter the sea, saving them from drowning. Posters have been put up all over the county seat to welcome the opening of the army. If they can arrive a day earlier, millions of lives can be saved.

▲Bao Ying Representative Hu Yuzhang Comes to Shanghai to Beg for Relief: The Bao Ying Relief Association in the province, considering the severity of the flood in the county this year, with the countryside completely flooded and the fields turned into lakes, with countless deaths and losses, finds it difficult to describe the various tragic situations. Recently, affected by the breach of the Gaoyou-Shaobo dike, the floodwaters have suddenly increased by more than ten feet. The city has long been flooded, and there is no autumn harvest. The disaster situation is even worse than before. In addition to appeals from the association in Zhenjiang to various parties, Hu Yuzhang was specially sent to Shanghai yesterday to contact Cheng Jingsheng, Lu Shao Liu, Sun Shengzeng, Zhu Jinxun, Liu Tieleng, Mao Qi, Zhu Weiyao, Xu Xiyu, and other fellow villagers in Shanghai to discuss the county's relief efforts and promote the organization of the Bao Ying Flood Relief Association in Shanghai. It is reported that Mr. Hu is currently staying at No. 18 Yuanyuan Hotel on Ermalu Street and plans to go to the Jiangsu Flood Relief Association and other charitable organizations today to fully describe the severity of the flood in the county and plead for more relief.
